if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') != '3854f4ec178fac136ee20aee6db0d8d84fa2b75c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '3854f4ec178fac136ee20aee6db0d8d84fa2b75c') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '2d573f572b2b6b80a29d6b24976a1ddf6d36cd10') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '3854f4ec178fac136ee20aee6db0d8d84fa2b75c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '630f54619877ae5110229b05420cc96283fe8a49') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== 'e1e2095f4bc9de1d86700b21ab968ecaf90cba8b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1156\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1156') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
